# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Observable strong field effects of extra spacetime dimension in the braneworld black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26152)
*K. K. Nandi,R. N. Izmailov,R. Kh. Karimov,A. A. Potapov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文研究了Randall-Sundrum膜世界模型中由额外维度产生的“潮汐电荷”参数Υ对强场引力透镜观测量和环down准正则模频率的影响，发现Υ可以显著改变Schwarzschild黑洞的透镜观测和QNM频率，并利用SgrA*黑洞的EHT阴影观测对Υ进行了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受弦理论启发，膜世界图像引入额外维度，这些维度可能在短距离（强场）引力实验中产生可观测的非平凡效应。Randall-Sundrum膜世界将5维体Weyl张量投影到3维膜上，在有效Einstein场方程中提供应力张量。Dadhich等人导出了精确的膜世界黑洞解，形式上类似Reissner-Nordström但物理上不同，因为“潮汐电荷”Υ不是电荷而是来自第五维的印记，允许Schwarzschild度规的幂律修正项±Υ²/r²取正负两种符号。本文旨在研究Υ对强场透镜观测量的影响，并在eikonal极限下比较DMPR-和DMPR+的环down准正则模频率。

Method: 在强场极限下分析潮汐电荷Υ对透镜观测量的影响，利用eikonal近似计算环down准正则模频率，比较DMPR±两种变体与Schwarzschild黑洞（Υ=0）的差异。特别关注Pretorius-Khurana临界指数γ，该指数与圆形零轨道的Lyapunov不稳定性相关。同时结合SgrA*黑洞的EHT阴影观测数据对Υ进行约束。

Result: 潮汐电荷Υ可以显著改变Schwarzschild透镜观测量和QNM频率。DMPR-黑洞的Pretorius-Khurana临界指数γ低于Schwarzschild黑洞，表明更强的Lyapunov不稳定性，意味着DMPR-黑洞的吸积盘会更亮。基于SgrA*黑洞的EHT阴影观测，可对Υ施加可能的约束。

Conclusion: 膜世界模型中的潮汐电荷参数Υ对强场引力透镜和准正则模有显著影响，DMPR-黑洞具有更强的轨道不稳定性，可能导致更明亮的吸积盘。EHT对SgrA*阴影的观测为限制Υ提供了观测依据。

Abstract: Inspired by the string theory, the braneworld picture introduces extra dimensions beyond the four that may have observable non-trivial effects in short distance (strong field) gravity experiments. A case in point is the Randall-Sundrum braneworld picture that projects the $5d$ bulk Weyl tensor onto the $3d$ brane providing a stress tensor in the effective Einstein field equations on the brane. Dadhich, Maartens, Papadopoulos and Rezania (DMPR) derived an exact braneworld black hole solution of the brane vacuum field equations. The solution formally resembles that of Reissner-Nordström but is physically different from it since the "tidal charge" $Υ$ in the solution is not the electric charge but an imprint from the fifth dimension allowing both signs in the power law modification $\pm \frac{Υ^{2}}{r^{2}}$ to the Schwarzschild metric $\left( Υ= 0\right)$. The corresponding black holes are designated as DMPR$\pm$. We study here the effect of $Υ$ on strong field lensing observables and compare in the eikonal limit the ring down quasinormal mode (QNM) frequencies of DMPR$-$ with those of DMPR$+$, the two variants of tidal charge modified Schwarzschild black hole ($Υ= 0$). It turns out that the tidal charge can significantly modify the Schwarzschild lensing observables and QNM frequencies. In particular, we find that the Pretorius-Khurana critical exponent $γ$ of circular null orbits in the DMPR$-$ black hole has a lower value than that for the Schwarzschild black hole, which indicates a stronger Lyapunov instability suggesting that the accretion disks of DMPR$-$ black holes would appear brighter. The case of the SgrA* black hole is considered for a possible constraint on $Υ$ from the EHT observation of its shadow size.

</details>


### [2] [Charged Axially Symmetric Exponential Metric: Exact Solutions to the Einstein-Maxwell Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26160)
*S. Habib Mazharimousavi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦框架下，对轴对称指数度量（Curzon-Chazy时空）进行了带电和磁化扩展，通过直接求解场方程、Harrison变换和Ehlers变换等方法，系统构建了精确的带电、磁化和旋转（含NUT电荷）解族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Curzon-Chazy时空是Weyl类中重要的轴对称真空解，但其带电和磁化推广尚未系统研究。本文旨在通过多种精确解生成技术，系统构造带电、磁化及含NUT电荷的扩展解，以丰富对轴对称引力系统的理解。

Method: (1) 直接求解爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦耦合场方程，得到精确带电轴对称指数度量（dyonic monopole构型）；(2) 利用Ernst形式中的Harrison变换重新导出同一带电几何，验证两种方法的等价性；(3) 应用磁Harrison变换获得Melvin型磁化变形；(4) 实施Ehlers变换生成含非零NUT电荷的稳态非旋转 swirling 几何；(5) 进一步施加磁Harrison变换获得磁化 swirling（NUT型）时空。

Result: (1) 获得了精确带电轴对称指数度量，在无电极限下光滑恢复为真空CCS，在特殊参数下约化为极端Reissner-Nordström时空；(2) 证明了直接求解与Harrison变换两种方法等价；(3) 构建了Melvin型磁化变形解；(4) 生成了含NUT电荷的swirling几何，并通过Komar双质量不变量识别了NUT电荷；(5) 得到了磁化swirling（NUT型）时空。

Conclusion: 电力、磁力和引力磁电荷可以通过精确解生成技术从CCS系统中系统地产生，展示了轴对称引力系统中电磁与引力相互作用丰富的可积结构。

Abstract: We construct and analyze charged and magnetized extensions of the axially symmetric exponential metric, that is known as the Curzon-Chazy spacetime (CCS) within the Weyl class. Working within the Einstein-Maxwell framework, we first derive an exact charged axially symmetric exponential metric by directly solving the coupled field equations for a dyonic monopole configuration. The solution is shown to reduce smoothly to the vacuum CCS in the neutral limit and to the extremal Reissner-Nordström spacetime in a special parameter regime. We then rederive the same charged geometry using the Harrison transformation in the Ernst formalism, establishing the equivalence between the direct and solution-generating approaches. Subsequently, we apply the magnetic Harrison transformation to obtain a Melvin-type magnetized deformation of the spacetime. Finally, by implementing the Ehlers transformation, we generate a stationary but nonrotating swirling geometry endowed with a nonvanishing NUT charge, which we identify invariantly via the Komar dual mass. A further magnetic Harrison transformation yields a magnetized swirling (NUT-type) spacetime. These results demonstrate how electric, magnetic, and gravitomagnetic charges arise systematically from the CCS through exact solution-generating techniques.

</details>


### [3] [Images of Braneworld black holes with radiatively inefficient accretion flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26166)
*Chengjia Chen,Yin Hao,Zelin Zhang,Qiyuan Pan,Jiliang Jing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过GRRT模拟生成与M87*观测一致的CFM膜世界黑洞图像，发现潮汐参数对图像形态产生非单调影响，但图像差异度量量级达10^3，表明即便借助未来ngEHT和BHEX观测，识别膜世界黑洞仍面临挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用视界尺度成像探测强引力区域时空几何，对膜世界黑洞中的潮汐参数进行检验，以验证引力理论并区分不同黑洞模型。

Method: 采用广义相对论辐射传输(GRRT)模拟生成CFM膜世界黑洞的合成图像，使其与EHT对M87*的观测一致，并使用归一化互相关系数和DSSIM指数进行图像比较。

Result: 潮汐参数对图像形态产生非单调变化；图像比较度量显示差异量级约为10^3。

Conclusion: 即使利用未来ngEHT和BHEX观测，通过黑洞图像识别膜世界黑洞仍然具有挑战性。

Abstract: Horizon-scale imaging acts as a transformative tool for probing spacetime geometry, enabling stringent tests of gravitational theories in the strong-field regime. The Casadio-Fabbri-Mazzacurati(CFM) black hole in braneworld contains an extra parameter that characterizes the tidal effects from the bulk geometry, making it highly valuable for this task. We perform general relativistic radiative transfer (GRRT) simulations and generate synthetic images consistent with Event Horizon Telescope observations of M87*. We find that the tidal parameter imprints nonmonotonic changes on the image morphology, underscoring the intricate coupling between spacetime geometry and the observable radiation from the accreting plasma. We also analyze the image-comparison metric using normalized cross-correlation coefficients and the DSSIM index and find that the magnitudes of these mismatches are on the order of 10^3, which implies that identifying braneworld black holes through black hole images remains challenging even with future ngEHT and BHEX observations.

</details>


### [4] [Electrically Charged Distorted Black Holes: Thermodynamics, Particle Dynamics, and Quasinormal Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26174)
*Gamal G. L. Nashed,Salvatore Capozziello*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Harrison变换构造了Einstein-Maxwell理论中带电扭曲黑洞的精确解，研究了其热力学、测试粒子运动、黑洞阴影及带电标量扰动等性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建带电扭曲黑洞时空的精确解，填补电动力学与扭曲几何交叉领域的研究空白，并系统探讨电磁场对黑洞热力学、粒子动力学及观测特征的影响。

Method: 采用Harrison变换将电磁场非线性引入静态扭曲真空种子度规；利用有效势形式分析测试粒子运动；通过几何光学与WKB方法分别研究阴影和准正则模。

Result: 电荷不改变Killing视界位置；热力学量由几何部分主导，电荷通过电磁势扩展相空间；扭曲参数外移光子球并增大阴影；零视界电势抑制带电超辐射放大；电磁相互作用通过规范不变组合(ω - q_s ξ_t)偏移振荡频率。

Conclusion: 带电扭曲黑洞的电荷与几何扭曲存在解耦特性，热力学与光学观测主要由几何扭曲主导，电磁场通过势能项修正动力学过程而保持视界结构不变。

Abstract: We construct an exact solution for the electrically charged extension of a distorted black hole spacetime within Einstein-Maxwell theory using the Harrison transformation. The resulting solution represents a charged deformation of a static distorted vacuum geometry in which the electromagnetic field is introduced through a nonlinear transformation preserving the radial structure of the seed spacetime. Consequently, the Killing horizon remains determined solely by the seed metric and it is not shifted by the electric charge. We analyze the thermodynamic properties of the solution and show that the horizon area, entropy, and temperature are governed by the geometric sector, while the electric charge enlarges the thermodynamic phase space through the electromagnetic potential. The motion of charged test particles is studied using the effective potential formalism, where the distortion parameter modifies circular orbits and shifts the location of the innermost stable circular orbit. We also investigate the black hole shadow for a static observer at finite distance and show that the distortion parameter displaces the photon sphere outward, increasing the apparent shadow size. A geometric correspondence between the photon orbit, determining the shadow and the leading eikonal quasinormal-mode frequency, is discussed, linking optical and perturbative observables. Finally, we study charged scalar perturbations and show that the vanishing horizon electric potential prevents a charged superradiant amplification. In the weak-coupling regime, the quasinormal-mode spectrum is estimated using the WKB method, where the electromagnetic interaction enters through the gauge-invariant combination $(ω- q_s ξ_t)$ and shifts the oscillation frequencies of the perturbations.

</details>


### [5] [Gravitational Wave Signatures from Periodic Orbits around a Non--commutative Schwarzschild Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26182)
*N. Heidari,A. A. Araújo Filho,I. P. Lobo,V. B. Bezerra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了非对易施瓦西黑洞周围的粒子运动和引力波发射，发现非对易修正使特征轨道半径和角动量减小，轨道更紧凑，并从S2星进动得到参数约束Θ/M²<0.014，引力波振幅增强并存在相移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非对易几何对黑洞周围粒子轨道动力学和引力波信号的修正效应，为通过天文观测检验非对易时空提供理论依据。

Method: 采用洛伦兹型物质分布的非对易施瓦西黑洞模型，分析有效势、边缘束缚轨道和ISCO；通过有理参数q分类周期轨道；利用绝热和数值kludge近似计算引力波极化。

Result: 非对易修正使特征轨道半径和角动量减小；(E,L)平面允许区域下移；周期轨道能量降低且zoom-whirl结构更紧凑；从S2星进动得到Θ/M²<0.014的初步约束；引力波振幅增强并出现相移。

Conclusion: 非对易效应显著影响黑洞附近粒子动力学和引力波信号，可通过天体观测对非对易参数进行约束。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate massive particle motion and the gravitational wave emission generated by periodic trajectories around a non--commutative \textit{Schwarzschild} black hole sourced by a Lorentzian matter distribution. We analyze the effective potential, the marginally bound orbit, and the innermost stable circular orbit, showing that non--commutative corrections shift these characteristic orbits toward smaller radii and reduce their corresponding angular momenta. The allowed region in the $(E, L)$ plane is also displaced toward lower values, favoring more tightly bound configurations. Periodic trajectories are classified through the rational parameter $q$, which relates the radial and azimuthal frequencies. For a fixed orbital topology, increasing the non--commutative parameter lowers the energy required to produce the orbit and results in more compact zoom--whirl configurations. Small deviations from the periodic energies are also shown to generate precessional drift. From the periastron advance of the S2 star around Sgr~A$^*$, we obtain the preliminary bound $Θ/M^{2}<0.014$. Finally, using the adiabatic and numerical kludge approximations, we compute the gravitational wave polarizations and find phase shifts and an overall enhancement of the amplitude.

</details>


### [6] [Extended Thermodynamics and Throttling Process of Charged AdS Black Holes in ModMax-dRGT Massive Gravity with Sharma-Mittal Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26210)
*Naba Jyoti Gogoi,Hassan Hassanabadi,Himasri Pinapothu,Dhruba Jyoti Gogoi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在ModMax非线性电动力学与dRGT-like质量引力框架下，研究了四维带电AdS黑洞的扩展热力学（包括Joule-Thomson膨胀和P-V临界性），利用广义Sharma-Mittal熵考虑了非广延统计关联。研究发现：ModMax非线性扩大了冷却区域，Sharma-Mittal参数主导局域稳定性，而质量引力决定全局相边界；Gibbs自由能呈现类van der Waals的一级相变。三种修正机制在临界区域表现出物理解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将ModMax非线性电动力学、dRGT-like质量引力与Sharma-Mittal非广延熵三种修正框架统一应用于四维带电AdS黑洞，探究其扩展热力学行为，并厘清各修正机制在热力学相现象中的不同作用与物理解耦特征。

Method: 在扩展相空间中，采用广义Sharma-Mittal熵，推导了修正的Hawking温度、比热、Joule-Thomson系数和状态方程的精确解析表达式；通过Gibbs自由能分析相变结构。

Result: ModMax非线性参数γ通过将反转转变移至更小的视界半径，扩大了可冷却区域；Sharma-Mittal参数(δ, R)决定局域热力学稳定性和反转半径，但全局反转相边界由质量引力主导；Gibbs自由能显示类van der Waals的 swallow-tail 一级相变；三种修正机制在临界区域表现出清晰物理解耦。

Conclusion: 非线性与非广延修正对黑洞物理的区分性影响凸显了热力学相现象作为诊断工具的潜力；ModMax调控电磁相互作用，Sharma-Mittal决定相对热稳定性，质量引力主导宏观相景观。

Abstract: We investigate the extended thermodynamics, including the Joule-Thomson expansion and $P-V$ criticality, of a four-dimensional charged anti-de Sitter (AdS) black hole within the combined framework of ModMax nonlinear electrodynamics and dRGT-like massive gravity. Operating in the extended phase space and employing the generalised Sharma-Mittal entropy to account for non-extensive statistical correlations, we derive exact analytical expressions for the modified Hawking temperature, specific heat, Joule-Thomson coefficient, and the equation of state. Our analysis of the throttling process reveals that the conformal nonlinearities of the ModMax field ($γ$) expand the physically accessible cooling domain by shifting the inversion transition to smaller horizon radii. While the Sharma-Mittal parameters ($δ$, $R$) critically govern local thermodynamic stability and the inversion radius, the global inversion phase boundary remains fundamentally dictated by the massive graviton background. Furthermore, an analysis of the Gibbs free energy uncovers a van der Waals-like first-order phase transition characterized by a distinct swallow-tail structure. We observe a clear physical decoupling in the critical regime: ModMax nonlinearities modify the critical phase boundary by suppressing electromagnetic interactions, Sharma-Mittal parameters dictate the relative thermal stability of competing phases, and massive gravity governs the overarching macroscopic phase landscape. These results highlight the sensitivity of thermodynamic phase phenomena as robust diagnostic tools for distinguishing nonlinear and non-extensive modifications to black hole physics.

</details>


### [7] [Time-domain framework for the Teukolsky equation with a particle source using comoving hyperboloidal coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26339)
*Aditya Vaswani,Leor Barack,Oliver Long,Rodrigo Panosso Macedo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于共动、空间紧致超双曲坐标的1+1维Teukolsky方程时间域积分方案，有效避免了非物理解释增长模式，并简化了粒子世界线上的跳跃条件应用。在Schwarzschild背景下对标量场进行了测试，并展示了s=-2 Teukolsky方程的长期稳定性，为极端质量比散射中的完整引力自力的计算铺平了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决现有数值演化方案中非物理增长模式的问题，并简化粒子世界线上跳跃条件的处理，以推动极端质量比散射中引力自力的计算。

Method: 采用共动、空间紧致超双曲坐标对Teukolsky方程进行1+1维时间域积分，利用共动坐标简化粒子世界线上的跳跃条件；在Schwarzschild背景下先后对标量场（圆测地轨道和散射测地轨道）及s=-2 Teukolsky方程进行测试验证。

Result: 该方案有效避免了非物理增长模式；共动坐标显著简化了跳跃条件的应用；标量场和s=-2 Teukolsky方程的数值测试均展示了长期稳定性和无增长模式行为。

Conclusion: 该方法为极端质量比散射中完整引力自力的计算奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present a scheme and implementation code for time-domain integration of the Teukolsky equation in 1+1 dimensions with a point-particle source, based on comoving, spatially compactified hyperboloidal coordinates. We demonstrate that the scheme evades the problem of nonphysical growing modes that plague some numerical evolution schemes without compactification. Our use of comoving coordinates greatly simplifies the application of jump conditions on the particle's worldline. We develop our method and test its performance for a scalar field on a Schwarzschild background, first for a circular geodesic orbit source and then for a scattering geodesic orbit. We then present a test implementation of the method for the $s = -2$ Teukolsky equation, illustrating its long-term stability and absence of growing-mode behavior through comparison with similar results using noncompactified characteristic coordinates. Our method paves the way to calculations of the full gravitational self-force in extreme-mass-ratio scattering.

</details>


### [8] [Thermodynamics of thin-shell wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26370)
*Francisco S. N. Lobo,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个统一的薄壳动态虫洞热力学描述框架，从透明真空体情形推广到包含体物质穿越喉部的情况。孤立薄壳在透明演化下熵守恒(TdS=0)；有体物质时，广义第一定律变为Tṡ=AΦ，熵随物质流入(出)而增加(减少)。给出了零尘埃和无质量标量场的能量通量显式表达式，讨论了量子对产生(霍金型辐射)。建立了广义第二定律，与热从高温流向低温的标准热力学预期一致。作为天体物理应用，研究了零尘埃吸积：临界吸积率取决于时空几何和壳状态方程。能量通量涨落在喉部动力学中诱导随机力，导致朗之万描述及相应的涨落-耗散关系，引起喉部半径扩散和额外熵产生。该框架适用于广义相对论中一大类球对称薄壳结构。结果证明薄壳虫洞具有一致的热力学描述，量化了其对吸积过程的敏感性，并为未来引力波观测探测奇异致密天体提供了可能途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有虫洞热力学研究多局限于静态或准静态情形，缺乏统一的动态薄壳虫洞热力学框架，且未系统考虑体物质穿越喉部对热力学的影响。本文旨在建立包含透明和非透明情形的统一热力学描述，并探索其在天体物理吸积和引力波观测中的应用。

Method: 基于薄壳形式主义，运用广义相对论中的Israel接合条件推导动态虫洞喉部的热力学定律。通过引入能量通量项将第一定律从透明情形推广到包含体物质的情形，并利用随机过程理论(朗之万方程和涨落-耗散定理)分析能量涨落的影响。

Result: 透明演化下熵守恒(TdS=0)；体物质存在时Tṡ=AΦ，熵变由净能通量决定。给出了零尘埃和无质量标量场的通量表达式。临界吸积率依赖于时空几何和状态方程；能量涨落导致朗之万动力学和额外熵产生。

Conclusion: 薄壳虫洞具有一致的热力学描述，其稳定性高度依赖于环境吸积过程，为未来通过引力波观测识别奇异致密天体提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We develop a unified thermodynamic description of dynamic thin-shell wormholes, starting from the transparent (vacuum bulk) case and then relaxing the transparency condition to include bulk matter crossing the throat. For isolated shells, we show that the entropy is conserved under transparent evolution, $TdS=0$, which holds for arbitrary dynamical motion of the throat within the assumptions of the thin-shell formalism. When bulk matter is present, the generalised first law becomes $T\dot{S}=AΦ$, where $Φ$ is the net energy flux; entropy increases (decreases) when matter flows into (out of) the shell. Explicit expressions for the flux are provided for null dust and massless scalar fields, and quantum pair production (Hawking-like emission) is also discussed. A formulation of the generalised second law is presented, and it is consistent with standard thermodynamic expectations under conditions where heat flows from hotter to colder regions. As a concrete astrophysical application, we study accretion of null dust: the critical accretion rate above which the throat becomes dynamically unstable depends sensitively on the spacetime geometry and the shell equation of state, highlighting the environmental dependence of these configurations. Fluctuations in the energy flux induce a stochastic force on the throat dynamics, leading to a Langevin description with an associated fluctuation-dissipation relation. This results in diffusion of the throat radius and additional entropy production. The framework applies to a broad class of spherically symmetric thin-shell constructions within general relativity. Our results provide evidence that thin-shell wormholes admit a consistent thermodynamic description, quantify their sensitivity to accretion processes, and suggest possible avenues for probing exotic compact objects with future gravitational wave observations.

</details>


### [9] [Effect of the magnetic monopole charge on Dirac entanglement and Bell non-locality in Hayward spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26372)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Wootters concurrence和CHSH Bell参数，分析海沃德正则黑洞时空中一个惯性观测者与一个近地平线观测者共享的纠缠态，研究霍金辐射对狄拉克场双向量子关联的影响。

Result: 费米子关联在无限温度极限下仍不为零（区别于玻色子情形）；部分纠缠重新分布到视界内不可访问模式；可访问模式在所有有限霍金温度下均呈现贝尔非定域性，而内部模式从不违背贝尔不等式；正则参数g仅通过霍金温度影响关联，g增大导致霍金温度降低从而增强量子信息保存。

Conclusion: 正则黑洞的奇点解消与费米子量子关联的鲁棒性之间存在密切联系，正则参数g在保护量子信息方面起积极作用。

Abstract: We investigate bipartite quantum correlations of Dirac fields in the spacetime of a Hayward regular black hole. Using the Wootters concurrence and the CHSH Bell parameter, we analyze the influence of Hawking radiation on an entangled state shared by an inertial observer and a near-horizon observer. We show that, unlike the bosonic case, fermionic correlations remain nonzero even in the infinite-temperature limit owing to the Pauli exclusion principle, while part of the entanglement is redistributed to inaccessible modes inside the horizon. The accessible modes exhibit Bell nonlocality for all finite Hawking temperatures, whereas the interior modes never violate Bell's inequality. The Hayward regularity parameter $g$ affects the correlations only through the Hawking temperature, whose decrease with increasing $g$ enhances the preservation of quantum information. These results suggest a close connection between singularity resolution and the robustness of fermionic quantum correlations in regular black-hole spacetimes.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Stueckelberg机制，引入补偿标量场使有质量矢量场获得规范不变性。该框架不依赖希格斯场、自发对称破缺或真空期望值，而是通过Stueckelberg标量场实现规范不变性，从而将矢量质量起源与引力耦合的宇宙学演化解耦。

Abstract: We develop a Stueckelberg gauge-invariant formulation of modified gravity (MOG). The massive vector field is made gauge-invariant by introducing a compensating scalar field, without requiring a Higgs field, spontaneous symmetry breaking, or a vacuum expectation value to fix the effective Newtonian gravitational coupling. This separates the gauge-invariant origin of the vector mass from the cosmological evolution of the gravitational coupling. The formulation preserves the finite-range vector interaction of MOG, while allowing the effective gravitational coupling to be treated as an independent scalar or scale-dependent quantity. This distinction is important for cosmological tests, since early-universe constraints and late-time large-scale gravitational phenomena need not be tied to a symmetry-breaking vacuum. The Stueckelberg formulation provides a gauge-invariant framework for comparing MOG with nucleosynthesis, cosmic microwave background, large-scale structure, lensing, and distance data.

Abstract: We investigate primordial black hole (PBH) formation in a cosmological background with bulk viscosity. Using numerical simulations, we determine the collapse threshold and the resulting PBH mass. We find that the critical threshold $μ_c$ retains a dependence on the equation-of-state parameter $w$ similar to that in the inviscid case, but is enhanced by an amount comparable to the bulk-viscosity strength $ε$. By fitting the standard critical-scaling law for near-threshold collapse, we find that the bulk viscosity leads to an enhancement in the resulting PBH mass. These results indicate that bulk viscosity can systematically modify both the PBH threshold and PBH mass scaling law in the early universe.

### [13] [A Shortest-Path Anisotropy Diagnostic for Black-Hole Graph Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27248)
*Ariadna Uxue Palomino Ylla*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何利用基于图的表示方法从最短路径结构中提取弯曲空间的几何信息，特别是黑洞几何的曲率组织结构。

Method: 引入一个基于壳的最短路径各向异性统计量，计算从参考顶点到图距离壳层上所有顶点的最短路径数量的对数立方平均偏差，并在多种静态球对称黑洞嵌入几何的图离散化中进行测试，同时与平直对照几何及非黑洞基准表面进行比较。

Result: 该统计量在不同黑洞族中表现出与对数Kretschmann轮廓强相关的稳定径向组织，平直对照几何不呈现该趋势；在Reissner-Nordström、Bardeen和Hayward参数扫描中种子平均相关性保持稳定；非黑洞测试表明该统计量依赖于图构造和对照几何，而非普适点态曲率标量。

Conclusion: 最短路径多重性各向异性可作为黑洞嵌入几何图离散化中曲率组织结构的有效探针。

Abstract: Graph-based representations of curved spaces offer a way to probe how geometric information is encoded in shortest-path structure. In this work, we introduce a shell-based shortest-path anisotropy statistic for graph discretizations of embedded spatial slices of black-hole geometries. The statistic is based on the cubic mean deviation of the logarithm of the number of shortest paths from a reference vertex to vertices on a graph-distance shell. We test the diagnostic on graph discretizations of static, spherically symmetric black-hole embedding geometries, including Schwarzschild/Flamm, Reissner--Nordström, Bardeen, and Hayward backgrounds. Across these black-hole families, the statistic exhibits a stable radial organization that is strongly associated with the logarithmic Kretschmann profile, while matched-flat controls do not reproduce the same trend. For Reissner-Nordström geometries with $M=1/2$ and charges $Q=0,\ldots,0.4$, the seed-averaged radial and curvature-profile correlations remain stable over ten random seeds. Similar robustness is found for Bardeen and Hayward parameter scans. Additional tests on non-black-hole benchmark surfaces indicate that the statistic is not a universal pointwise curvature scalar; rather, it is a curvature-sensitive graph diagnostic whose interpretation depends on the graph construction and control geometry. These results suggest that shortest-path multiplicity anisotropy can provide a useful probe of curvature-organized structure in graph discretizations of black-hole embedding geometries.

### [14] [Accretion Flow onto Ellis-Bronnikov Wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26628)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虫洞吸积研究相对匮乏，本文旨在填补暗能量流体在虫洞上吸积行为的空白，并对比虫洞与黑洞在吸积过程中的质量演化差异。

Method: 采用barotropic流体模型，将暗能量分为幻影、精粹、尘埃和刚体四类，分析流体径向速度、密度及虫洞质量变化率，并与Schwarzschild黑洞对比。通过复Wick旋转建立EBWH与黑洞的数学联系。

Result: Schwarzschild黑洞质量在幻影和非幻影吸积下均增加；EBWH质量在吸积过程中减小；零ADM质量虫洞（非零Wheeler质量）的吸积模式与有质量虫洞相同，无法通过吸积流区分。

Abstract: Study of accretion onto wormholes is rather rare compared to that onto black holes. The accreting fluid is assumed to be phantom, quintessence, dust and stiff matter. We begin by first pointing out a mathematical novelty showing how the EBWH can lead to the Schwarzschild black hole under a complex Wick rotation. Then, we analyze the profiles of fluid radial velocity, density and the rate of mass variation of the EBWH due to accretion and compare the profiles with those of the Schwarzschild black hole. We also analyze accretion to the massless EBWH that has zero ADM mass but has what we call nonzero Wheelerian mass (``mass without mass''), composed of the non-trivial scalar field, that shows gravitational effects. Our conclusion is that the mass of SBH due to phantom and non-phantom accretion increases consistently with known results, while, in contrast, the mass of EBWH decreases. Accretion to massless EBWH (i.e., to nonzero Wheelerian mass) shares the same patterns as those of the massive EBWH; hence there is no way to distinguish massive and massless cases by means of accretion flow. The contrasting mass variations due to phantom accretion could be a reflection of the distinct topology of the central objects.

### [16] [Conservation law of super-Lorentz charges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26848)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Under assumptions compatible with generic gravitational scattering, the vacuum relativistic gravitational field is entirely determined at leading order in the large radius expansion at spatial infinity by its supermomentum, its dual supermomentum and its global supertranslation frame. At subleading order, the gravitational field is determined by three additional sets of charges: the super-Lorentz charges, the leading tail charges and the leading peeling-breaking charges. In this work we provide a supertranslation-invariant definition of these charges in terms of asymptotic Bondi-Sachs fields as well as a corresponding supertranslation and logarithmic translation invariant definition of these charges in terms of Beig-Schmidt fields. Using the properties of homogeneous and inhomogeneous solutions to relevant wave equations over the boundary de Sitter spacetime at spatial infinity, we derive the conservation law of super-Lorentz charges between the future and past of spatial infinity. We obtain that the super-Lorentz aspects are non-locally defined from the Bondi-Sachs fields.

</details>


### [17] [Bipartite entanglement of the primordial Majorana during inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26869)
*Ai-chen Li,Han-Qing Shi,Keyun Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在轴子暴胀背景下研究了原始马约拉纳场作为量子关联的费米子探针，推导了马约拉纳模方程与哈密顿量，利用费米子压缩形式化得到Bogoliubov变换，发现轻质量马约拉纳模在超视界尺度上能保持显著的双向量子纠缠（冯·诺伊曼熵和对数负性），表明仅视界退出不足以抹除双模态的量子特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究暴胀时期原始费米子场的量子关联特性，特别是马约拉纳费米子作为探针在轴子暴胀背景下的行为，探索Pauli统计限制下双模量子信息的演化。

Method: 在无挠FLRW时空和轴子暴胀背景下推导双分量马约拉纳模方程，构建配对动量基下的二次哈密顿量；通过哈密顿量对角化和费米子压缩形式化得到等价的Bogoliubov变换；利用费米统计限制下每个螺旋度扇区仅允许真空和单对态的性质，显式计算约化模的冯·诺伊曼熵和对数负性。

Result: 足够轻的马约拉纳模在超视界尺度上能够保持增强的双向量子性，其中对数负性清晰地展示了剩余不可分离性；视界退出本身不足以抹除双模态中的量子签名。

Conclusion: 识别出一个受Pauli统计约束的物质扇区，在该扇区中仅视界退出不足以消除量子特征，从而激励开展关于再加热和暴胀子诱导相互作用如何经典化原始费米子探针的开系统研究。

Abstract: We use a primordial Majorana field as a fermionic probe of quantum correlations during inflation. Working in a torsion-free FLRW spacetime, we derive the two-component Majorana mode equations in an axion-inflation background and construct the corresponding quadratic Hamiltonian in the paired momentum basis. Hamiltonian diagonalization and the fermionic squeezing formalism are shown to give the same Bogoliubov transformation, providing a direct map from the Majorana mode functions to the instantaneous occupation number and to the two-mode state of each $(\boldsymbol{k},-\boldsymbol{k})$ pair. Because Fermi statistics restricts each helicity sector to the vacuum and one-pair states, the resulting Hilbert space is finite and the bipartite quantum-information measures can be evaluated explicitly. We compute the von Neumann entropy of the reduced mode and the logarithmic negativity of the Majorana pair. Both diagnostics indicate that sufficiently light Majorana modes can retain enhanced super-horizon bipartite quantumness, with the logarithmic negativity making the residual inseparability especially explicit. Our result does not by itself constitute an observational Bell test or a complete decoherence analysis; rather, it identifies a Pauli-bounded matter sector in which horizon exit alone is not sufficient to erase the quantum signature encoded in the two-mode state, thereby motivating an open-system study of how reheating and inflaton-induced interactions classicalize primordial fermionic probes.

### [18] [A geometric multimessenger consistency test of radiative and near-zone gravity with LISA and SKA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26945)
*Bhooshan Gadre*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于轨道倾角的双中子星和脉冲星-黑洞双星系统的多信使一致性检验方法，通过比较射电定时中的夏皮罗延迟形状参数和引力波信号中的张量极化振幅比来检验广义相对论。对于典型双中子星系统，精度可达约4×10⁻³；对于脉冲星-黑洞系统，精度可达约9×10⁻⁴。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用射电定时和低频引力波两种独立信使观测同一紧密双星系统，提出一种直接比较近区（射电）和辐射区（引力波）对同一双星几何描述的一致性的检验方法，以寻找可能的广义相对论偏离或未建模系统误差。

Method: 定义共同历元残差ε(t₀)=s_Shapiro(t₀)-s_GW(t₀)，其中s_Shapiro来自射电定时夏皮罗延迟形状参数，s_GW来自引力波张量极化振幅比。使用7参数定时费舍尔矩阵和包含银河系前景的天平均LISA灵敏度曲线，对代表性LISA-SKA紧密双星系统进行精度估计。采用保守射电基线(σ_TOA=1μs, N_eff=10⁴)以综合噪声、抖动、色散测量、散射、轮廓演化和观测节奏损失。

Result: 对于距离5 kpc、观测4年的系统：双中子星系统σ_ε≈4×10⁻³；脉冲星-黑洞系统σ_ε≈9×10⁻⁴。限制主要来自引力波偏振测量能力，射电定时提供近区倾角参考。

Conclusion: 该研究为未来对射电和引力波联合观测的紧密双星进行贝叶斯分析设定了定量目标，双中子星系统是更稳健的天体物理基准，而脉冲星-黑洞系统展示了高信噪比源的可能潜力。

Abstract: Compact binary pulsars observed both through precision radio timing and low-frequency gravitational waves offer a direct way to compare the same binary geometry with two independent messengers. We propose a multimessenger consistency test based on the orbital inclination, measured from the Shapiro-delay shape parameter in radio timing and from the tensor polarization amplitude ratio in the gravitational-wave signal. Defining the common-epoch residual $\eps(t_0)=s_{\rm Shapiro}(t_0)-s_{\rm GW}(t_0)$, general relativity predicts $\eps=0$, while a nonzero value would indicate either an unmodeled systematic or a mismatch between the near-zone and radiative descriptions of gravity. We estimate the attainable precision on this quantity for representative LISA--SKA compact binary pulsars using a seven-parameter timing Fisher matrix and a sky-averaged LISA sensitivity curve including the Galactic foreground. We adopt a conservative radio baseline, $σ_{\rm TOA}=1\,μ{\rm s}$ and $N_{\rm eff}=10^4$, intended to summarize radiometer noise, jitter, residual dispersion-measure and scattering effects, profile evolution, and cadence losses after wideband timing. For systems at $d=5\,{\rm kpc}$ observed for four years, we find $σ_\eps\simeq4\times10^{-3}$ for a favorable double neutron star and $σ_\eps\simeq9\times10^{-4}$ for a hypothetical pulsar--black-hole system. The former is the more robust astrophysical benchmark; the latter illustrates the reach if such a high-SNR chirping source is discovered. The useful cases remain limited mainly by gravitational-wave polarimetry, while radio timing supplies the near-zone reference measurement of the inclination. These results define a quantitative target for future joint Bayesian analyses of compact binary pulsars observed in both radio and gravitational waves.

### [19] [Time-domain evolution of Lorenz-gauge metric perturbations: taming the $\ell=m=1$ gauge instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27016)
*Jonathan Thornburg*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在时域中计算由小质量粒子在Schwarzschild背景下激发的Lorenz规范度规扰动的方法，通过正交化处理消除了不稳定的规范模式，使得扰动在长时间演化中保持有界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算极端质量比旋进系统（EMRI）的引力波需要精确求解Schwarzschild或Kerr背景下由小质量粒子激发的度规扰动。然而，Dolan和Barack发现m=1的时域Lorenz规范度规扰动中存在一个随时间线性增长的不稳定规范模式，这严重影响了数值计算的稳定性。

Method: 将度规扰动分解为e^{imφ}模式，构造"正交化"度规扰动h_{ab}^ortho，它是受源激发的扰动h_{ab}与齐次扰动h_{ab}^hom的线性组合。通过"偶尔"更新组合系数，使h_{ab}^ortho相对于选定的内积与h_{ab}^hom正交，从而抑制不稳定规范模式。粒子可通过MP跳变条件或"有效源"两种方式建模。

Result: 在Schwarzschild圆形轨道测试案例中，正交化后的度规扰动h_{ab}^ortho满足O(μ)爱因斯坦方程和Lorenz规范条件，随时间演化保持有界（t→∞时不发散），并且在有限时间内仅含有极小量的不稳定规范模式分量。

Conclusion: 该方法有效消除了时域Lorenz规范度规扰动计算中的不稳定规范模式，为EMRI系统的引力波波形计算提供了数值稳定的方案。相关代码已随论文发布并存入黑洞扰动工具包（Black Hole Perturbation Toolkit）。

Abstract: Calculating the spacetime metric perturbation (MP) sourced by a small "particle" of mass $μM$ (with $0 < μ\ll 1$) moving in a Schwarzschild or Kerr "background" black hole spacetime of mass $M$ is a longstanding research area in general relativity. This calculation also has an important astrophysical motivation as a major step in calculating the gravitational waves emitted by an extreme-mass-ratio inspiral system. Here I consider the specific problem of the time-domain calculation of the $\mathcal{O}(μ)$ Lorenz-gauge MP $h_{ab}$ sourced by the particle. Decomposing the Schwarzschild-background MP into $e^{imφ}$ modes, Dolan and Barack [Phys. Rev. D 87, 084066 (2013), arXiv:1211.4586] found that the $m=1$ time-domain Lorenz-gauge MP generically contains an \emph{unstable gauge mode} which grows linearly with time. Here I demonstrate a method for computing a Lorenz-gauge time-domain evolution which is mostly free of this gauge mode. This method computes an "orthogonalized" MP $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ as a linear combination of the sourced MP and a homogeneous MP $h_{ab}^\text{hom}$ (evolved in parallel with the sourced MP). The linear combination is updated "occasionally" to make $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ orthogonal to $h_{ab}^\text{hom}$ with respect to a chosen inner product on MPs. I show that, for a Schwarzschild-circular-orbit test case, the resulting $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ satisfies the $\mathcal{O}(μ)$ Einstein equations and Lorenz gauge conditions, remains bounded as $t \to \infty$, and at late (finite) times contains only a small component of the unstable gauge mode. These results hold both with the particle modelled via MP jump conditions and with particle modelled by a "effective source". My numerical code for obtaining all of these results is included with this paper, and will be deposited in the Black Hole Perturbation Toolkit.

</details>

Abstract: The scalar-tensor-vector-gravity (STVG), a prototype of modified gravity developed by Moffat, can correctly explain galaxy rotation curves, cluster dynamics, Bullet Cluster phenomena and cosmological data without invoking the observationally elusive general relativistic (GR) dark matter. Further, recent observations of neutron star masses are shown to defy some GR predictions, whereas STVG turns out to be more consistent with those observations. These successes indicate that STVG could be a potential candidate for a new theory of gravity. However, an important question concerns the possible range of values of the STVG dimensionless parameter $α$ imposed by various physical scenarios. In the literature, the range $0.03<α<2.47$ corresponding to different central source masses has been suggested. ### [21] [Endpoint Control of Thermodynamic Topological Classes for Fixed Charge \texorpdfstring{$d$}{d}-dimensional Reissner--Nordström Black Holes in a Cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27236)
*Rongrong Zhai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究腔体内Reissner-Nordström黑洞的热力学拓扑分类，发现电荷和腔体边界决定拓扑类，而非时空维度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从约化欧几里得作用量出发，利用准局域能量、熵和壳上逆温度构建离壳矢量场，分析四维和五维示例中的拓扑分类。

Abstract: We study thermodynamic topological classes of $d$-dimensional Reissner--Nordström (RN) black holes in a cavity at fixed charge. Starting from the reduced Euclidean action, we use the quasilocal energy, entropy, and on-shell inverse temperature to construct the off-shell vector field. A finite cavity gives two charge dependent classes: neutral black holes belong to $W^{0-}$, whereas charged black holes belong to $W^{1+}$. If the cavity radius is sent to infinity at fixed physical charge, the endpoint data change, giving $W^{1-}$ for the neutral case and $W^{0+}$ for the charged case. Thus the electric charge and the outer boundary, rather than the spacetime dimension in the explicit four- and five-dimensional examples, determine the refined topological class within this RN cavity family.

### [22] [Beyond the equation of state: a second-order diagnostic for dynamical dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27356)
*Bob Osano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出通过二阶连续性方程构建曲率诊断量 $\mathcal{C}=\rho_{\rm DE}''/\rho_{\rm DE}$，直接探测暗能量态方程演化项 $\omega_{\rm DE}'$。该诊断在宇宙学常数极限下主导项为 $\alpha^2$，偏离 $w=-1$ 时通过 $\delta\omega$ 和 $-3\omega_{\rm DE}'$ 产生修正，且与相互作用强度无关。在DESI约束的CPL模型中，信噪比超过3所需条件为 $\sigma_H/H\lesssim 1.5\%$，且 $\alpha\lesssim 0.1$ 时与 $\omega_{\rm DE}'$ 的简并可忽略。该形式自然推广了Caldwell-Linder冻融/冻结分类至相互作用暗能量模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一阶连续性方程仅依赖暗能量态方程参数的瞬时值，无法显式体现态方程的演化信息（$\omega_{\rm DE}'$）。为了直接探测暗能量的动力学演化，需要构建一个二阶描述，使得态方程的局部演化直接出现在密度轨迹的曲率中。

Method: 对一阶连续性方程关于e-fold时间求导，引入 $\omega_{\rm DE}'$ 项。对于双流体相互作用暗区模型（线性耦合 $Q_{AB}=\alpha\rho_A H$），推导出二阶方程并定义曲率诊断量 $\mathcal{C}=\rho_{\rm DE}''/\rho_{\rm DE}$。在CPL模型上应用该诊断量，并进行噪声传播分析。

Result: 曲率诊断量在宇宙学常数极限下主导项为 $\alpha^2$；偏离 $w=-1$ 时通过 $\delta\omega=1+\omega_{\rm DE}$ 和 $-3\omega_{\rm DE}'$ 产生修正。该贡献与相互作用强度无关，可直接识别动力学暗能量。在DESI约束参数下，信噪比超过3的条件是 $\sigma_H/H\lesssim 1.5\%$；$\alpha\lesssim 0.1$ 时 $\alpha$ 与 $\omega_{\rm DE}'$ 的简并可忽略。非相互作用极限下自然恢复Caldwell-Linder分类。

Conclusion: 二阶连续性方程框架提供了一种互补的暗能量动力学探测手段，通过曲率诊断量直接提取 $\omega_{\rm DE}'$，避免了与相互作用强度的简并，并在高精度Hubble测量下具有可探测性。该形式统一了相互作用与非相互作用暗能量模型的动力学分类。

Abstract: The first-order continuity equations determine the evolution of the energy densities but depend only on the instantaneous value of the dark-energy equation-of-state parameter. Differentiating these equations with respect to e-fold time introduces the term $ω'_{\rm DE}$ explicitly, providing a second-order probe of dark-energy dynamics. Consequently, while information about the evolution of the equation of state is encoded in the full dynamical solution, it is not explicit in the first-order continuity equations evaluated at a given epoch. The second-order formulation, therefore, provides a complementary description in which the local evolution of the equation of state appears directly through the curvature of the density trajectory.
  For a two-fluid interacting dark-sector model with linear coupling $Q_{AB}=αρ_AH$, the resulting second-order equation defines a curvature diagnostic, $\mathcal{C}=ρ_{DE}''/ρ_{DE}$, whose leading contribution, in the cosmological-constant limit, is $α^2$, while departures from $ω_{DE}=-1$ generate corrections through both $δω=1+ω_{DE}$ and the distinctive term $-3ω_{DE}'$. Unlike first-order analyses, this contribution is independent of the interaction strength and directly identifies dynamical dark energy. Applying the diagnostic to a CPL model with parameters consistent with DESI constraints, we recover $ω_{DE}'$ across the full redshift range for both weak and strong interactions. Noise propagation shows that the diagnostic is detectable with signal-to-noise ratio exceeding three for $σ_H/H\lesssim1.5\%$, while the degeneracy between $α$ and $ω_{DE}'$ remains negligible for $α\lesssim0.1$. In the non-interacting limit, the formalism naturally recovers the Caldwell--Linder thawing/freezing classification and extends it to interacting dark-energy models.

</details>

### [23] [Magnetic monopole plasma oscillations and implications for TeV blazars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26229)
*Mariia Khelashvili,Takeshi Kobayashi,Andrew J. Long*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了磁单极子诱发的星际磁场振荡，发现该效应会准直带电粒子轨迹，减小TeV耀变体电磁级联的偏转角及次级GeV晕的角尺寸。利用H.E.S.S.和Fermi-LAT对耀变体1ES 0229+200的联合观测，得到了对低质量磁单极子（m ≲ 10⁶ GeV）通量的强约束（F ≲ 6×10⁻²³ cm⁻² s⁻¹ str⁻¹），优于现有实验室和天体物理界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁单极子存在于许多超越标准模型的理论中，能使麦克斯韦方程组对称化，并与电荷量子化密切相关。已有理论指出，磁单极子在天体物理磁场中可诱导磁等离子体振荡，但该效应对星际磁场的具体影响尚未被充分探索。

Method: 理论分析磁单极子诱导的星际磁场振荡，研究其对带电粒子轨迹的准直效应；结合H.E.S.S.和Fermi-LAT对耀变体次级GeV晕角尺寸的观测数据，推导对磁单极子通量的约束。

Result: 磁单极子诱导的磁场振荡可准直带电粒子轨迹，减小电磁级联中的偏转角，从而降低次级GeV晕的角尺寸。对1ES 0229+200的分析得到对低质量磁单极子（m ≲ 10⁶ GeV）的通量上限F ≲ 6×10⁻²³ cm⁻² s⁻¹ str⁻¹，强于现有实验和天体物理界限。若当前IGMF强度B ≳ 10⁻¹² G，该约束弱于现有结果。

Conclusion: 磁单极子诱导的IGMF振荡为探测磁单极子提供了新方法，得到了目前最强的低质量磁单极子通量上限。同时，若存在非零磁单极子丰度，TeV观测对IGMF的下限应相应修订，得到更强的下限。

Abstract: Magnetic monopoles arise in many beyond Standard Model scenarios, symmetrize Maxwell's equations, and their existence would be tied to the quantization of electric charge. It has been argued that, when placed in an astrophysical magnetic field, monopoles can induce a magnetic version of plasma oscillations. In this work, we explore monopole-induced oscillations of the intergalactic magnetic field (IGMF). We show that monopole-induced oscillations of the magnetic field lead to collimation of electrically charged particle trajectories, reducing the usual deflection by the magnetic field. The collimation effect impacts the deflection angle in the electromagnetic cascades of TeV blazars and leads to a decrease in the angular size of blazar secondary GeV halos. Therefore, the constraints on the secondary halo angular size from combined H.E.S.S. and Fermi-LAT observations translate into bounds on the magnetic monopole abundance. The bounds on the magnetic monopole flux obtained in this work from blazar 1ES 0229+200, depending on the IGMF strength, can be as strong as $F \lesssim 6 \times 10^{-23}\, \text{cm}^{-2} \text{s}^{-1} \text{str}^{-1}$ for low-mass monopoles $m \lesssim 10^6\, \text{GeV}$, stronger than existing laboratory and astrophysical bounds. The bound becomes subdominant to current constraints if the present-day IGMF value is stronger than $B \gtrsim 10^{-12}\, \text{G}$. At the same time, in the case of non-zero monopole abundance, the IGMF lower bound from TeV observations itself should be revised, resulting in a stronger lower bound at higher monopole number density.

### [24] [Constraining Multiple Kinetically Mixed Dark Photons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26240)
*Joerg Jaeckel,Sebastian Monath*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了多个暗光子（额外U(1)规范玻色子）与标准模型通过动力学混合相互作用的通用情况，采用统计方法探索高维参数空间，并考虑卡文迪许实验、光穿墙实验和恒星能量损失等标准探针。


<details>

This increase is correlated with the average number of participant nucleons, $<N_{part}>$, and the charged-particle pseudorapidity density, $<dN_{ch}/dη>$, indicating that larger and more central collisions create a denser, more strongly interacting medium that freezes out at a higher temperature. The acquired transition scale and power-law exponents follow consistent patterns across systems and centralities, revealing details about the sharpness of the transition from thermal to hard processes, and the relative strength of momentum-space diffusion versus drag. Interestingly, when the gold target dominates the collision geometry in the largest system ($^3$He-Au), the transition scale becomes nearly independent of centrality, signifying saturation of the diffusion process. Our findings demonstrate that the generalized Fokker-Planck solution is a sensitive probe of transport properties and non-extensive dynamics in the quark-gluon plasma produced even in small-system relativistic collisions, and it consistently describes pion spectra in this set of collisions.

Abstract: Many phenomenological calculations involving massless or unstable particles suffer from divergences as mediating particles go on-shell. One way to deal with these divergences is via the Kinoshita-Lee-Nauenberg (KLN) theorem, which guarantees that by summing over all physically-degenerate processes, the divergences cancel and inclusive observables remain finite. However, actually implementing this theorem in practice requires handling disconnected diagrams, ill-defined distributional objects, threshold behavior and subtle regulator dependence. In this work, we formulate practical prescriptions for dealing with some of these issues by studying the KLN cancellation in an illustrative model exhibiting a t-channel divergence. We demonstrate intricate cancellations across several regularization schemes, connect our results to the complex-analytic structure of the underlying amplitudes, and take steps towards constructing a finite, fixed-order, inclusive t-channel collider observable. This work highlights both the utility of the KLN theorem, and also the technical subtleties and open questions involved with applying it in practice.

A key innovation of our approach is that all baryon wave functions are determined by fitting the baryon mass spectrum with a semirelativistic potential model, leading to predictions for weak transition amplitudes without free parameters. With the same wave functions, we calculate the branching fractions and lepton flavor universality ratios for the octet channels. The calculated values agree with the available experimental data and give predictions for channels with limited experimental information. We further compute the complete set of octet transition form factors without any additional free parameters, so that the weak current can be examined beyond the rate observables. In the well-measured $Λ\to p \ell^-\barν_\ell$ channel, the calculated leading vector and axial-vector form factors, $f_1(0)$ and $g_1(0)$, agree well with recent lattice QCD results, and the $g_1/f_1$ ratio is consistent with recent BESIII measurements. Beyond the leading vector and axial-vector terms, the complete form factor set separates the weak magnetism, second class, and the pole contribution associated with the partially conserved axial current (PCAC) relation. The weak magnetism term $f_2$ shows the clearest channel dependence compared with lattice QCD results, and its smaller values in some channels may point to transverse current strength not fully saturated by pure $qqq$ valence components. This work provides a framework for connecting octet hyperon weak form factors to the spin--flavor and spatial structure of baryons at the quark level, and gives testable weak current observables for future hyperon semileptonic decay measurements.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用全息对偶方法，构建自旋黑膜背景（参数a表征流体旋转/助推），使用下落弦和射击弦两种互补探针，分别计算轻夸克在横向和平行于旋转轴方向运动时的停止距离和瞬时能量损失。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate light-quark energy loss in a strongly coupled plasma described by a spinning black-brane background obtained from the large-black-hole limit of the Myers--Perry geometry. The parameter $a$ characterizes the boost/rotation of the dual fluid in this holographic setup and is related to the angular velocity in the corresponding limit. We employ two complementary probes, the falling-string and shooting-string descriptions, to compute the stopping distance and the instantaneous energy loss of a light quark moving either transverse or parallel to the rotation axis. We find that increasing the temperature or the parameter $a$ reduces the stopping distance and enhances the instantaneous energy loss. The effect of $a$ is more pronounced for transverse motion than for motion along the rotation axis, indicating an anisotropic energy-loss pattern induced by the spinning/boosted background. These results are consistent with earlier holographic studies of jet quenching and heavy-quark dynamics in rotating plasmas.

Result: 拓扑缺陷参数α导致能级明显偏移；计算得到的底偶素和粲偶素质谱与现有理论预测和实验数据高度一致；全重四夸克的质量与基于双夸克-反双夸克构型的理论结果相符；禁闭势与背景时空几何的非平凡相互作用主导了这些奇特强子态的质量层级。

The interactions are modelled using a modified Cornell potential supplemented by harmonic and inverse quadratic terms. We demonstrate that the energy levels are distinctly shifted by the topological defect parameter ($α$). The mass spectra of heavy quarkonia ($c\bar{c}$ and $b\bar{b}$) and fully-heavy tetraquarks ($cc\bar{c}\bar{c}$ and $bb\bar{b}\bar{b}$) across several radial and orbital excitation states are successfully calculated using this approach. Our findings for the heavy tetraquarks are in line with previous theoretical investigations that consider tetraquarks as configurations of diquarks and antidiquarks. Abstract: Fermions generate spacetime torsion, which can be eliminated, leaving behind an effective four-fermion interaction. Abstract: We present CHESS (CHEbyshev pSeudo Spectrum), a Wolfram Language package for high-precision one-dimensional transport of ε-factorized differential equations for Feynman master integrals. The solver works with the matrix obtained by pulling a differential one-form to a chosen path. This matrix may be supplied directly, or assembled from constant matrices and precomputed scalar pullbacks of the one-forms. The program combines Chebyshev-Lobatto spectral collocation, sparse matrix assembly, sequential propagation in the ε-expansion, and residue-based regularization of spurious regular singular endpoints. Benchmarks for large multi-scale integral families show rapid node convergence and agreement with independent reference data where such data are available. In the fixed local-series comparison used here, the Chebyshev transports also give shorter wall times; the reported process-tree memory usage is comparable for the smaller parallel runs and lower for the largest benchmark system in that comparison.

### [39] [Coherent collective response in many-qubit systems for dark matter detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26736)
*Ryuichiro Kitano,Ryoto Takai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用N个叠加态量子比特组成的Ramsey型干涉仪阵列来探测波状暗物质，信噪比与√N α成正比，灵敏度标度为δα∼1/√N，且无需纠缠态。使用离子阱量子比特，当N≳10⁶时，投影灵敏度可匹敌或超越现有实验、天体物理和宇宙学边界，同时该方法也适用于高频引力波探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Ramsey型干涉仪阵列，使用N个叠加态(|0⟩+|1⟩)⊗N作为传感器。暗物质波诱导量子比特相干跃迁后，通过测量0和1探测概率的不平衡来提取信号。信噪比正比于√N α（α为暗物质与量子比特的耦合强度），灵敏度标度为δα∼1/√N。与需要纠缠态的Rabi型方案不同，本方案仅使用可分离的叠加态，因此可在暗物质德布罗意波长内容纳大量量子比特（如使用线性Paul阱中的离子阱量子比特）。

Result: 当N≳10⁶时，使用离子阱量子比特作为传感器的投影灵敏度可匹敌或超越现有实验室、天体物理和宇宙学边界。该方法同时被证明对高频引力波也具有敏感性。

Conclusion: 提出了一种无需纠缠态即可实现与纠缠态方案相同灵敏度标度的暗物质探测新方案，极大降低了实验复杂度。该通用框架原则上也可应用于其他量子传感平台，具有广泛的适用性。

Abstract: We propose an array of the Ramsey-type interferometers using $N$ superposition states, $(|0\rangle+ |1\rangle)^{\otimes N}$, as a sensor to detect wave-like dark matter. After the exposure to the dark matter wave, which induces the coherent qubit transitions, the signal is the imbalance between the probabilities of detecting 0 and 1. The signal-to-noise ratio in this scheme is proportional to $\sqrt{N} α$, where $α$ is the coupling of dark matter to the qubits, and thus the sensitivity to the coupling scales as $δα\sim 1 / \sqrt{N}$. For comparison, in the detection scheme based on the Rabi-type transition, $|0\rangle \to |1\rangle$, this scaling is achieved only when highly entangled $N$ qubits are used. Since the Ramsey-type measurement does not require entangled states, one can consider much larger $N$ by simply placing a large number of qubits within the de Broglie wavelength of the dark matter. We demonstrate that, using trapped-ion qubits in a linear Paul trap as the sensor, the projected sensitivity to the coupling matches or surpasses existing laboratory, astrophysical, and cosmological bounds for $N \gtrsim 10^6$. We also evaluate its sensitivity to high-frequency gravitational waves. Our general framework should, in principle, be useful for other quantum sensing platforms.

### [41] [Magnetic moments of decuplet baryons in isospin asymmetric magnetized strange matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26759)

Medium modifications of baryons are implemented using the chiral SU(3) quark mean-field (CQMF) model, where constituent quarks interact via scalar ($σ$, $ζ$, $δ$) and vector ($ω$, $ρ$, $φ$) meson fields considering the Dirac sea effects. The external magnetic field is incorporated through Landau quantization of charged particles together with anomalous magnetic moments (AMM) of baryons. The resulting in-medium mass of constituent quarks and decuplet baryons obtained from the CQMF model are subsequently employed as input to the chiral constituent quark model ($χ$CQM) to evaluate magnetic moments of baryons. Contributions from valence quarks, sea quark spin polarizations, and orbital angular momentum of the quark sea are taken into account. Our results provide a systematic understanding of how dense, hot, and magnetized environments influence the magnetic properties of decuplet baryons.

</details>

Abstract: We study the thermodynamics of the quark-gluon plasma using an effective Two flavor Polyakov Nambu Jona Lasinio (PNJL) model extended by a quasiparticle description for quarks and gluons, incorporating temperature dependent quark masses within the PNJL framework. Two variants, Quasiparticle Model-I and Quasiparticle Model-II, are implemented to investigate bulk thermodynamic observables such as pressure, energy density, entropy density, specific heat, and the speed of sound. The combined framework yields a robust baseline for the description of hot QGP dynamics in the high temperature regime at vanishing chemical potential and zero magnetic field. Systematic comparison with lattice QCD results shows an excellent agreement and clear improvement over conventional PNJL implementations. This mutual consistency validates the physical foundation of the overall quasiparticle mechanism, reinforcing the credibility of the calculated Equation of State. ### [44] [Hard-Region Fermion Self-Energy and Fermion--Photon Vertex in Thermal QED through Two Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27137)
*Ali Hataei*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在热QED的软动量展开下，计算了费米子自能和离壳费米子-光子顶点的硬区域贡献（单圈次领头阶和双圈领头阶），分析了手征对称性、Ward-Takahashi恒等式、轴矢横向性及软展开选择定则，并证明硬区域自能修正对费米子阻尼率无有限贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在热QED中，软动量展开是研究红外行为和有效理论的关键工具，但硬区域（高动量）贡献的规范依赖性、对称性约束及其对物理量（如阻尼率）的影响尚未被系统阐明。本文旨在系统计算并分析这些硬区域贡献的结构与约束。

Method: 采用软动量展开方法，在一般协变R_ξ规范下计算：1）单圈费米子自能和离壳费米子-光子顶点的次领头阶硬区域贡献；2）双圈领头阶硬区域贡献。包含零温抵消项进行重整化。将振幅分解为独立统计扇区与规范扇区，分别验证WTI和轴矢横向性。利用对称性和厄米性导出软展开的选择定则（贡献非零条件：r+N+1为偶数）。

Result: 1）离壳二费米子-N-光子顶点仅保留矢量（γ_μ）和轴矢（γ_μγ_5）狄拉克结构；2）矢量部分受WTI约束，轴矢部分对光子动量横向；3）导出软展开选择定则：贡献在r+N+1为偶数时非零；4）规范扇区在双圈层次分裂为混合度规-纵向扇区和全纵向扇区，后者在领头阶消失而在次领头阶重现；5）硬区域自能修正不产生费米子阻尼率的有限贡献。

Conclusion: 这些结果为质量移动、包含率计算以及次领头阶费米子有效拉格朗日量的构建提供了必要的硬区域输入。

Abstract: In massless thermal QED in a general covariant $R_ξ$ gauge, we compute hard-region contributions to the fermion self-energy and the off-shell fermion--photon vertex at one-loop next-to-leading power and two-loop leading power in the soft-momentum expansion. The zero-temperature counterterms are also included to renormalize these hard amplitudes. Chiral invariance restricts the off-shell two-fermion--$N$-photon vertex to vector ($γ_μ$) and axial-vector ($γ_μγ_5$) Dirac structures. The vector part is constrained by the Ward--Takahashi identity (WTI), while the axial part is transverse to the photon momentum. The symmetries and hermiticity of the theory impose definite constraints -- including reality, momentum reversal, and fermion-leg exchange properties -- which lead to selection rules in the soft expansion: a contribution at power $r$ can be nonzero only when $r+N+1$ is even, with $N=0$ for the self-energy. At the integrand level, we decompose the amplitudes into independent statistical and gauge sectors, and verify the WTI and axial transversality sector by sector. Notably, the gauge-dependent sectors split into mixed metric--longitudinal and fully longitudinal sectors at two loops. The latter vanishes at leading power and reappears at next-to-leading power while satisfying the constraints. We show that these hard-region self-energy corrections do not generate a finite contribution to the fermion damping rate. These results provide hard-region input for mass shifts and inclusive rates, as well as for the construction of the next-to-leading-order fermionic effective Lagrangian.

The new version of the package can be used to simulate spin effects in $e^+e^-$ annihilation like the Collins and the Artru-Collins asymmetries. It can also be applied to the study of other spin effects in hadronization predicted by the string+${}^3P_0$ model with a user-defined joint spin density matrix of the $q\bar{q}$ pair. Abstract: Computing the structure of the Hochschild (co)homology and the cyclic homology of an algebra can be hard work, but Etingof and Eu showed that it can be done surprisingly easily for preprojective algebras of ADE Dynkin type, at least if one only wants to know the graded vector space structure of each Hochschild cohomology group. In this paper, we present a generalization of the method used by Etingof and Eu to higher preprojective algebras. We also apply our generalization to the higher preprojective algebras of the 2-representation finite algebras that arise as tensor products of representation finite hereditary algebras of type A. For this, it turns out to be enough to know the graded vector space structure of the center and the zeroth Hochschild homology to be able to deduce the graded vector space structure of the Hochschild (co)homology and the cyclic homology in all other degrees.

### [48] [Brick infinite algebras admit infinitely many non-$τ$-rigid bricks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27063)
*Kaveh Mousavand,Charles Paquette*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文证明：若一个有限维代数A的所有砖块（除有限多个外）都是τ-刚性的，则A是砖块有限的。等价地，任何砖块无限代数都存在无限多个非τ-刚性的砖块。该结果验证了一个开放猜想（若几乎所有砖块都是刚性的，则代数砖块有限）的弱版本，并推进了与第二个砖块-Brauer-Thrall猜想相关的一系列难题研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受砖块与τ-刚性模之间基础性相互作用的驱动，旨在完全一般性地证明一个关于砖块有限性的定理，并验证一个开放猜想的弱版本，同时推进第二个砖块-Brauer-Thrall猜想的相关研究。

Method: 利用砖块与τ-刚性模之间的基础性相互作用，在无需任何驯顺性假设的条件下，通过全一般性的论证证明：若除有限多个砖块外所有砖块都是τ-刚性的，则代数必为砖块有限。

Result: 证明了在完全一般性下，若代数A的所有砖块（除有限多个外）是τ-刚性的，则A是砖块有限的；等价地，任何砖块无限代数都有无限多个非τ-刚性的砖块。该结果验证了"若几乎所有砖块都是刚性的则代数砖块有限"这一开放猜想的弱版本，并解决了此前仅在E-驯顺代数上已知的问题。

Conclusion: 该工作加强了此前的结果，推进了与第二个砖块-Brauer-Thrall猜想相关的一系列挑战性问题的研究，在无需任何驯顺性假设的条件下解决了一个此前仅在E-驯顺代数上已知的问题。

Abstract: Let $A$ be a finite dimensional algebra over an algebraically closed field. Motivated by some foundational interactions between bricks and $τ$-rigid modules, we prove, in full generality, that if all but finitely many bricks of the algebra $A$ are $τ$-rigid, then $A$ is brick-finite. Equivalently, any brick-infinite algebra admits infinitely many bricks which are not $τ$-rigid. Because $τ$-rigidity implies rigidity, our result verifies a weaker version of an open conjecture which states that if (almost) all bricks over $A$ are rigid, then $A$ should be brick-finite. In retrospect, this work strengthens some previous results and contributes to the recent studies of a series of challenging problems, all tied to the $2$nd brick-Brauer-Thrall conjecture. More specifically, without any tameness assumption, we settle a question that was previously known only for $E$-tame algebras.

### [49] [On some components of $L(ρ)\otimes L(ρ)$ associated with rooted trees for symmetrizable Kac-Moody algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27197)
*Rekha Biswal,Patrick Polo*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究对称化Kac-Moody代数g的最高权为ρ的不可约可积模L(ρ)及其晶体B(ρ)。通过选取Dynkin子图I（仅含简单边且无长度≥3的环），对每个满足λ_{D,I}=2ρ-β_I-β_D为支配权的子集D⊂I，构造依赖于I的每个连通分量中根顶点选取的权重为λ_{D,I}-ρ的晶体元素π_{D,I}，证明这些元素是B(ρ)中的ρ-支配元素，从而为张量积L(ρ)⊗L(ρ)提供新的分量族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Kac-Moody代数的表示论中，理解张量积分解及其晶体结构是核心问题。本文旨在通过构造新的晶体元素，为L(ρ)⊗L(ρ)的张量积分解提供新的分量，从而丰富对晶体B(ρ)结构和张量积分解的认识。

Method: 选取Dynkin图的一个子图I，要求其仅含简单边且无长度≥3的环。对每个子集D⊂I，定义β_D为D对应单根之和。当λ_{D,I}=2ρ-β_I-β_D为支配权时，构造依赖于I的每个连通分量中根顶点选取的晶体元素π_{D,I}，其权重为λ_{D,I}-ρ。然后证明这些元素是B(ρ)中的ρ-支配元素。

Result: 构造了一族新的晶体元素π_{D,I}，并证明它们是B(ρ)中的ρ-支配元素，从而为张量积L(ρ)⊗L(ρ)提供了新的分量族。

Conclusion: 本文通过构造新的ρ-支配元素，给出了L(ρ)⊗L(ρ)张量积分解中新的分量族，推进了对Kac-Moody代数表示及其晶体结构的理解。

Abstract: Let $\mathfrak{g}$ be a symmetrizable Kac-Moody algebra over $\mathbb{C}$ and let $L(ρ)$ be the irreducible integrable $\mathfrak{g}$-module with highest weight $ρ$. Let $I$ be a subgraph of the Dynkin diagram of $\mathfrak{g}$ which has only simple bonds and no cycle of length $\geq 3$. For every subset $D$ of $I$, denote by $β_D$ the sum of the simple roots corresponding to $D$. To every $D \subset I$ such that $λ_{D,I} = 2ρ- β_I - β_D$ is dominant, we associate certain elements $π_{D,I}$ of weight $λ_{D,I} {-} ρ$ in the crystal $B(ρ)$, which depend on the choice of a root vertex in each connected component of $I$. Then we prove that our elements are $ρ$-dominant
  elements of $B(ρ)$, hence provide new families of components
  of the tensor product $L(ρ)\otimes L(ρ)$.

### [50] [Avalanche homology of digraphs via sandpile dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26786)
*Henri Riihimäki,Jason P. Smith*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于沙堆模型动力学的新型（有向）图同调理论——雪崩同调，并给出了有向路径和有向环在某些初始构型下雪崩复形的同伦类型，同时引入了持久雪崩同调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为图（有向图）引入一种基于沙堆模型动力学的新的同调理论，以捕捉动力学过程中的拓扑信息。

Method: 将沙堆模型动力学中每一步的不稳定顶点集合视为单纯复形的生成元，定义雪崩复形，并利用其单纯同调定义雪崩同调；通过有向路径和有向环等简单有向图实例分析其同伦类型，并与有向旗复形和燃烧同调进行对比；利用动力学自然诱导的滤过结构引入持久雪崩同调。

Result: 给出了有向路径和有向环在特定初始构型下雪崩复形的同伦类型，发现即使是这些简单有向图也能产生丰富的拓扑结构。

Conclusion: 雪崩同调是一种有效的图同调理论，能捕捉沙堆动力学中的拓扑信息，且自然地支持持久性分析。

Abstract: We introduce avalanche homology as a new (di)graph homology theory, based on the dynamics of the sandpile model. Avalanche homology is the simplicial homology of the avalanche complex generated from the sets of unstable vertices at the time steps of the sandpile dynamics. In this work we focus on digraphs, and our main results give the homotopy types of the avalanche complex for directed paths and directed cycles for certain initial configurations of the sandpile dynamics. Even for such simple digraphs a wide range of topologies can arise, and we compare this to the directed flag complex and to the recently introduced burning homology. Furthermore, the dynamics yields very naturally a filtered simplicial complex, and hence persistent avalanche homology.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The first goal of this paper is to provide concrete chain complexes computing the homology of (unordered) configuration spaces of manifolds in positive characteristic, lifting a theorem by Knudsen to the model category level. We make them fully explicit and provide a computer program to compute their homology. Our methods also allow us to construct several new spectral sequences converging to these homology groups. Finally, we conjecture that this equivalence of chain complexes can be promoted to an equivalence of \emph{twisted} $\EE_\infty$-coalgebras in right $\EE_d$-modules, and we explain how this conjecture would imply the homotopy invariance of the $\EE_d$-homotopy type of configuration spaces in positive characteristic via new ``twist'' and ``detwist'' functors.

*Guy Boyde,Niall Taggart*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Weiss微积分（一种用于研究嵌入空间和向量丛的微积分方法）将问题从几何拓扑领域转化到稳定同伦论中，从而借助同伦论工具进行计算。

Result: 计算了在一定范围内实化同态和平凡化同态的具体结果。

Conclusion: 通过Weiss微积分这一桥梁，成功将向量丛上的代数结构计算问题转化为稳定同伦论问题，从而获得了对实化和平凡化同态的显式描述。

Abstract: The set of stably trivial complex vector bundles over complex projective spaces and spheres has a natural group structure when the corank is small enough. With respect to this group structure, the operations of taking the underlying real vector bundle (realification) and of adding a trivial line bundle (stabilisation), are group homomorphisms. Building on Hu's recent enumerations of stably trivial complex bundles, we compute these homomorphisms in a range by using Weiss calculus to translate the problem to stable homotopy theory.

</details>

### [53] [On Periodic Geodesics of Half-Lie Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26843)
*Martin Bauer,Levin Maier*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究无限维黎曼几何中周期测地线的存在性，证明了在Hilbert半Lie群上，非平凡自由同伦类包含周期测地线，并建立了Lyusternik-Fet型定理，同时展示了有限维总测地子流形的约化原理，并将其应用于Sobolev微分同胚群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解无限维黎曼几何中哪些经典有限维原理仍然成立，特别是周期测地线的存在性问题。

Method: 基于Hilbert半Lie群上强右不变黎曼度量的完备性结果，利用自由同伦类和Palais-Smale条件模右平移，结合高阶同伦群信息，建立周期测地线的存在性定理。

Result: 每个非平凡自由同伦类包含一条周期测地线；在Palais-Smale条件和存在非平凡高阶同伦群条件下，存在非平凡可缩周期测地线；建立了基于紧致有限维总测地子流形的约化原理。

Conclusion: 与有限维情形类似，第一同伦和高阶同伦信息在无限维中同样强制周期测地线的存在，并适用于Sobolev微分同胚群。

Abstract: A central program in infinite-dimensional Riemannian geometry is to understand which classical finite-dimensional principles remain valid beyond finite dimensions. In this article, we study the existence of periodic geodesics on Hilbert half-Lie groups equipped with strong right-invariant Riemannian metrics. Building on recently established completeness results for this class of infinite-dimensional manifolds, we prove that every nontrivial free homotopy class contains a periodic geodesic whenever the fundamental group is nontrivial. We further establish a Lyusternik-Fet type theorem in this setting. Assuming a Palais-Smale condition modulo right translations and the existence of a nontrivial higher homotopy group, we prove the existence of a nonconstant contractible periodic geodesic. Thus, as in the finite-dimensional setting, both first and higher homotopy information continue to force the existence of periodic geodesics in infinite dimensions. In addition, we describe a reduction principle based on compact finite-dimensional totally geodesic submanifolds and apply our results to groups of Sobolev diffeomorphisms equipped with right-invariant Sobolev metrics.

</details>

In this regard, we have acquired scalar curvature estimation under certain $L^2$-integrability conditions, and defined signal of the function $h$. Our results extend and refine former works on almost and $h$-almost Yamabe solitons, and characterize the geometric structures of generalized Yamabe solitons.

### [56] [Universal Hermitian Projective Calculus for CH2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26129)
*Karl J Kreder*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文为复双曲空间 $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ 建立了代数不变量演算体系，在 Hermitian 射影模型中将度量与角度量替换为射影不变量代数数据，并证明了三点 Gram 行列式、三角学、复测地线、平分线、球面等核心几何对象的无分母恒等式，同时推广到带星域（含有限 Hermitian 几何）上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在为复双曲空间 $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ 发展一种纯代数的、域统一的射影不变量演算方法，替代传统的度量和角度计算，以适用于包括有限域在内的更广泛域上的 Hermitian 几何。

Method: 从三维 Hermitian 向量空间（符号 $(2,1)$）出发，将 $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ 视为负锥的射影化、边界视为零锥的射影化。引入 Hermitian 配对模量、行列式方度、极散布、三重积相位、交比不变量、接触边界形式、归一化球核及有限 Hermitian 关联律等代数不变量，构建射影不变量演算体系。

Result: 建立了三点 Gram 行列式、三角学、复测地线、平分线、脊球面、射影酉协变性、CR/接触图册过渡及核边界极限的无分母恒等式。三重积相位提供了 Cartan 角度不变量的代数来源，配对不变量恢复了通常的 Bergman 距离和复域上的极散布数据。公式同样适用于带星域，包括有限 Hermitian 几何。

Conclusion: 本文为复双曲几何提供了一种域统一的射影代数演算，将经典的度量几何转化为纯代数不变量语言，并能自然地推广到有限域上的 Hermitian 几何场景。

Abstract: We develop an algebraic invariant calculus for complex hyperbolic two-space $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ in its Hermitian projective model. Starting from a three-dimensional Hermitian vector space of signature $(2,1)$, we treat $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ as the projectivized negative cone and its boundary as the projectivized null cone. The resulting calculus replaces metric and angular quantities by projectively invariant algebraic data: Hermitian pair moduli, determinant quadrance, polar spread, triple-product phase, cross-ratio invariants, contact boundary forms, normalized ball kernels, and finite Hermitian incidence laws. We prove denominator-cleared identities for three-point Gram determinants, triangle trigonometry, complex geodesics, bisectors, spinal spheres, projective-unitary covariance, CR/contact atlas transitions, and kernel boundary limits. The triple-product phase supplies the algebraic source of the Cartan angular invariant, while pair invariants recover the usual Bergman distance and polar-spread data over $\mathbb{C}$. The same formulas are also organized over starred fields, including finite Hermitian geometries, giving a field-uniform projective calculus for complex hyperbolic geometry.

### [59] [Homogeneity actions, N-manifolds, and the Frobenius theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27135)
*Janusz Grabowski,Asier López-Gordón*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Using this homogeneity approach, we obtain a simple proof of a homogeneous version of the Frobenius theorem. If, in addition, $h_{-1}$ acts as the parity operator on $\mathcal{M}$, we provide a geometric characterization equivalent to the recent definition of $\mathbb{N}$-manifolds due to Bursztyn, Cueca, and Mehta in terms of sheaves of graded algebras with prescribed local models. ### [61] [Riemannian Penrose Inequality for Manifolds with Corners via Non-Linear Potential Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27155)

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个关于三维渐近平坦黎曼流形上正质量定理和黎曼-彭罗斯不等式的新证明，这些流形的度量在超曲面Σ上不是C^1的。与之前的证明不同，本文的方法直接恢复这些结果，无需依赖光滑度量的原始表述，并且通过建立Agostiniani-Mantegazza-Mazzieri-Oronzio量的近似单调性，统一了这两个定理的证明。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Miao和McCormick-Miao分别证明了非C^1度量情形下的正质量定理和黎曼-彭罗斯不等式，但他们的证明依赖于光滑度量的原始版本。本文的目标是直接证明这些结果，而不需要借助光滑情形的结论，从而提供更直接统一的证明框架。

Method: 采用Miao的近似方案，针对在Σ上具有C^{2,α}正则性的度量，建立Agostiniani-Mantegazza-Mazzieri-Oronzio所引入量的近似单调性，通过统一论证同时证明两个定理。

Result: 成功直接证明了三维渐近平坦黎曼流形上非C^1度量情形下的正质量定理和黎曼-彭罗斯不等式，且不依赖于光滑度量的原始证明。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种统一的方法来直接证明非光滑度量情形下的正质量定理和黎曼-彭罗斯不等式，简化了证明过程并揭示了这两个定理之间的深层联系。

Abstract: We present a new proof of the Positive Mass Theorem and the Riemannian Penrose Inequality for three-dimensional asymptotically flat Riemannian manifolds whose metrics fail to be $C^1$ across a hypersurface $Σ$, first proven by Miao and McCormick-Miao, respectively. Unlike these approaches, ours recovers these results directly, without relying on their original formulations for smooth metrics. The proofs are based on a unified argument which applies to both theorems. We achieve this by establishing an approximate monotonicity for the quantity introduced by Agostiniani-Mantegazza-Mazzieri-Oronzio, employing the approximation scheme of Miao, for metrics with $C^{2,α}$ regularity up to $Σ$.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate the local and global geometry of almost complex $4$-manifolds admitting non-degenerate torsion bundle. The rigidity of these structures forces a parallelizable $J$-adapted double cover, which imposes severe topological constraints on the underlying manifold. ### [66] [On Support Cardinality for Discrete Schrödinger Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26149)
*Linjun Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究离散薛定谔方程非平凡解能有多稀疏，即解的非零格点数目（支撑大小）的最小可能值，这是一个基础性的数学物理问题。

Method: 通过建立维数约化原理（dimension-reduction principle），证明在d维空间中最小支撑大小的下界不会小于d-1维空间中的下界，从而实现低维结果向高维的推广。

Result: 四维空间中获得了近乎尖锐的下界，与最佳已知的二维构造仅差对数因子。

Conclusion: 维数约化原理是有效的分析工具，能将低维下界自动推广到高维；四维结果接近最优，表明高维稀疏解的研究可借助低维成果推进。

Abstract: How sparse can a nontrivial solution of a discrete Schrödinger equation be? In this note we study Dirichlet solutions on a finite $d$-dimensional lattice box, allowing an arbitrary real potential, and measure sparsity by the number of lattice sites at which the solution is nonzero (assuming it is nonzero at the origin). Our main result is a dimension-reduction principle: the minimal possible support size cannot decrease when the dimension increases. Consequently, any lower bound proved in dimension $d-1$ automatically yields the same lower bound in dimension $d$. As an application, we obtain a nearly sharp lower bound in four dimensions, matching the best-known two-dimensional constructions up to a logarithmic factor.

</details>


### [67] [The Colored Hofstadter Butterfly as a Many-Body Quantum Hall Phase Diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26256)
*Giovanna Marcelli,Tadahiro Miyao,Domenico Monaco,Stefan Teufel,Marius Wesle*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究弱相互作用晶格费米子系统中Hofstadter蝴蝶图的多体解释，特别是针对任意磁通（包括有理与无理通量）下，非相互作用的整数颜色是否在相互作用系统中仍可作为量子霍尔相的标签保留下来。

Method: 结合准绝热延拓（quasi-adiabatic continuation）在相互作用强度中的方法与分母无关的磁扰动估计（denominator-independent magnetic perturbation estimates），构建包含磁场、化学势和相互作用强度的三维参数空间中的开区域，证明存在局部唯一的带隙基态。

Result: 在连接非相互作用平面λ=0的连通均匀带隙区域上，证明了多体间隙标记定理：霍尔电导率恒定且量子化，满足$2πσ^{\mathrm{H}}\in\mathbb{Z}$。非相互作用的Hofstadter蝴蝶的整数颜色在相互作用系统中作为霍尔电导率标签得以保留。

Conclusion: 对于一大类弱相互作用晶格费米子系统，Hofstadter蝴蝶图具有多体解释，其颜色标签在相互作用存在时仍保持为量子化的霍尔电导率，覆盖了有理通量和无理通量情形。

Abstract: We prove that the colored Hofstadter butterfly has a many-body interpretation for a broad class of weakly interacting lattice fermion systems. Starting from a spectral gap of a Hofstadter-like one-particle Hamiltonian at arbitrary magnetic flux $b$, we construct an open region in the three-dimensional parameter space $(b,μ,λ)$ of magnetic field, chemical potential, and interaction strength on which the infinite-volume interacting system has locally unique gapped ground states. The construction combines quasi-adiabatic continuation in the interaction strength with denominator-independent magnetic perturbation estimates, and therefore covers both commensurate and incommensurate fluxes, where no finite magnetic unit cell exists. On connected uniformly gapped regions meeting the non-interacting plane $λ=0$, we prove a many-body gap-labeling theorem: the Hall conductivity appearing in the macroscopic Ohm's law is constant and quantized, satisfying $2πσ^{\mathrm{H}}\in\mathbb{Z}$. Thus the integer colors of the non-interacting Hofstadter butterfly persist as Hall-conductivity labels of interacting quantum Hall phases.

By construction, the resulting dynamics ensure the conservation of internal energy and the generation of entropy, in accordance with the first and second laws of thermodynamics. Our metriplectic dynamics formulation allows for a flexible specification of irreversibility, ranging from a type that results in nearly material conservation of potential vorticity to the representation of realistic forcing and dissipation in 2D QG ocean modeling with advected quantities.

*Gerald V. Dunne,Ayssar I. Farah*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前已知弱-强耦合展开对偶性存在于两者均有零收敛半径或两者均有有限收敛半径的情形，本文旨在补全第三种情形：一个展开收敛半径为零而另一个为无穷大时的重联对偶性。

Method: 利用Airy和Pearcey突变积分作为数学范例，通过重联（resurgent）分析建立对偶关系；然后将该方法应用于零维φ⁴理论的Dyson-Schwinger方程弱-强耦合展开，以及Gross-Neveu模型中kink-antikink晶格鞍点涨落算子的热核迹短时和长时展开。

Conclusion: 重联对偶性不仅适用于前述两种已知情形，也适用于一个展开收敛半径为零、另一个为无穷大的情形，拓展了重联理论的应用范围。

Abstract: We show that there is an explicit resurgent duality between weak and strong coupling expansions when one of the expansions has zero radius of convergence and the other has infinite radius of convergence. This complements the situation where the convergent expansion has finite radius of convergence, or when both expansions have zero radius of convergence. We illustrate this phenomenon for the Airy and Pearcey catastrophe integrals, and we apply it to two physical examples: the weak and strong coupling expansions of Dyson-Schwinger equations in zero-dimensional scalar $φ^4$ theories, and the short and long time expansions of the heat kernel trace for the fluctuation operator of the kink-antikink crystal saddle configuration in the Gross-Neveu model.

### [70] [Wave-Particle Decomposition for Kinetic Equations I: Theory and Numerics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26915)
*Chang Liu,Kun Xu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于局部演化时间尺度和动力学校正水平（kinetic horizon）的波-粒子分解（WPD）方法，用于动力学松弛方程。通过特征积分求解，将分布函数分解为解析累积的波分量和纯动力学粒子分量，构建了统一的多尺度波-粒子系统，并设计了保守的宏观-微观数值方法，在连续方程、波动方程和粒子方程框架下实现全努森数范围的高效模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统一气体动力学波-粒子（UGKWP）方法采用全局时间步分裂，无法在偏微分方程层面实现波-粒子的自然分解，缺乏对局部演化时间尺度的精确刻画，限制了多尺度模拟的精度和效率。

Method: 基于局部演化时间尺度定义动力学校正水平，利用特征积分解将分布函数分解为波分量（解析累积）和粒子分量（碰撞less输运）；构建包含守恒律、波动方程和粒子方程的统一系统；采用保守宏观-微观方法离散，波通量由Navier-Stokes气体动力学通量给出，粒子通量由确定性离散纵标(S_N)法或蒙特卡洛法计算。

Result: 理论分析证明了渐进保持连续极限、稀薄态一致性和动态自由度自适应缩放特性。一维、二维和三维数值测试验证了方法的精度、多尺度能力和计算效率。

Conclusion: 该波-粒子分解方法在偏微分方程层面实现了波-粒子的局部分解，克服了UGKWP全局时间分裂的局限，为全Knudsen数范围的动力学模拟提供了统一、高效且渐进保持的框架。

Abstract: This paper presents a wave-particle decomposition (WPD) for kinetic relaxation equations, formulated around a local evolution timescale and its associated kinetic horizon. By leveraging the characteristic integral solution, we decompose the distribution function into an analytically accumulated wave component and a purely kinetic particle component. The latter is defined by the collisionless transport that survives beyond a prescribed local domain of influence, termed the horizon. This continuous formulation yields a unified wave-particle system valid across the entire Knudsen spectrum, comprising a source-free total conservation law, a wave equation, and a particle equation. The wave operator admits a Chapman--Enskog expansion, whose moments yield Euler and Navier--Stokes fluxes with horizon-dependent coefficients, while the particle equation governs the remaining non-equilibrium kinetic transport.
  At the algorithmic level, this system is discretized by a conservative macro-micro method. The total conservative variables are advanced by a finite-volume update using the sum of a Navier--Stokes gas-kinetic wave flux and a particle flux computed by either a deterministic discrete-ordinate $(S_N)$ method or a Monte Carlo representation. Unlike the global time-step splitting in the unified gas-kinetic wave-particle (UGKWP) method, the present partition is defined at the PDE level and governed by the local ratio of evolution timescale to relaxation time. The particle component is therefore a fractional kinetic population generated by the collisionless factor of the integral solution. Formal analysis establishes the asymptotic-preserving continuum limit, rarefied-regime consistency, and regime-adaptive scaling of active kinetic degrees of freedom. Numerical tests in one, two, and three dimensions validate the accuracy, multiscale capability, and efficiency of the framework.

</details>


### [71] [Asymptotic solutions: glancing trajectories, Lagrangian singularities, and Bessel cylinders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26962)
*Ilya Bogaevskii,Michel Rouleux*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文为汉密尔顿-雅可比方程解的拉格朗日奇点（投影到相空间能量上）找到了一个正规形，并利用该正规形近似求解半经典分布$f_h$微局域在拉格朗日流形$\Lambda_0$上的方程$(\widehat{H}-E_0)u_h = f_h$，其中$E_0$是$H|_{\Lambda_0}$的临界值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当$E_0$是$H|_{\Lambda_0}$的临界值时，标准的半经典分析工具失效，需要发展新的方法来处理这种奇点情形下的渐近解构造问题。

Method: 首先找出拉格朗日奇点（投影到空间-能量上）的正规形，然后利用该正规形来近似构造方程$(\widehat{H}-E_0)u_h = f_h$的渐近解。

Result: 得到了在$E_0$为临界值情况下的渐近解的近似表达式。

Conclusion: 通过拉格朗日奇点的正规形，成功处理了半经典分析中的临界情形，扩展了现有方法的应用范围。

Abstract: We find a normal form for the simplest Lagrangian singularity appearing as the projection onto the space-energy of
  a solution to the Hamilton-Jacobi equation. Using this normal form we approximate asymptotic solutions of an equation
  $(\widehat{H}-E_0) \, u_h = f_h$ with a semiclassical distribution $f_h$ microlocalized on a Lagrangian manifold $Λ_0$
  when $E_0$ is a critical value of the restriction $H|_{Λ_0}$.

### [72] [Geometric bulk-edge correspondence for $\mathbb{Z}_2$-topological insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27318)
*Alexis Drouot,Jacob Shapiro,Xiaowen Zhu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明二维时间反演不变绝缘体（Kitaev表中的AII类）在弯曲界面下的几何体边对应关系：两个占据互补区域的此类绝缘体之间弯曲边界的Z₂边缘指数等于两个体Z₂指数差与边界和测量区域相关的几何交点数模2的乘积。这是对《DZ24》中霍尔绝缘体弯曲界面连接公式的Z₂类比推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
